Just want to say to anyone excited for this: it looks like one of those games that have a great premise and fans wanted for years, but I'm afraid it's going to be a big disappointment.  1. This doesn't look high budget at all. Barely any gameplay, only CGI that was probably outsourced to other studio, and the little gameplay that is there is only premade animations of dinosaurs with no mechanics.  2. It is extremely reliant on nostalgia to sell itself, I mean c'mon, does she really have to trip on the same spoon the kids dropped in the movie? They recreate too many shots from the film instead of being creative, if the entire game is like that it's going to be boring. They even reused John Hammond's lines straight from the movie.  3. Let's be honest, Dinosaurs aren't Xenomorphs. Anyone expecting Alien: Isolation level of scares are setting themselves up for disappointment. Mechanically it's going to be very hard to justify scares, considering dinosaurs are animals and should act in a more natural way. They can't do crazy stuff like grab you from the ceiling, and they only hunt for food so why would they go through the trouble of hunting just this one skinny lady instead of a delicious triceratops.  I hope for this to be good, big fan of JP and even JW, but the signs are bad.

Well, after seeing this announcement trailer, I definitely prefer Jurassic Park: Survival over Jurassic Park: The Game that was developed and published by Telltale Games and released for PlayStation 3, Macintosh, Microsoft Windows, and Xbox 360 on November 15, 2011.  I read on Wikipedia that Jurassic Park: Survival was intended to be developed by Savage Entertainment, published by Konami, and released for PlayStation 2, Xbox, Microsoft Windows, and GameCube on November 14, 2001, but it was canceled because Universal was dissatisfied with the game's progress, including its poor animations, and Savage Entertainment confirmed on November 5th that they were no longer working on the game due to conflicts of Vivendi-Universal not providing funding to Savage Entertainment. I hope I'm wrong, but I've been disappointed by the video game industry too many times to give them the benefit of the doubt.  Also from a lore perspective, someone being left behind makes no sense. Based on the trailer they are following the film continuity, which made it pretty clear there was nobody else on the island. I'm tired of these lazy writers retroactively adding characters where they don't fit, in this case another "forgotten" park worker like in Jurassic Park: The Game, Fallen Kingdom and Dominion. For example, a plane or ship could have crashed on the island during the storm, and you play the only survivor, awoken by the sound of the survivors helicopter leaving overhead. That T-Rex roar is one of the most memorable and iconic movie sounds from my childhood. Fun fact: the growl the tyrannosaurs make before they roar is actually the sound elephants used to communicate over long distances. We normally can‚Äôt hear it because it‚Äôs below our hearing range, but when elephants are recorded and the audio is pitched up by a few octaves, we can hear them rumbling to each other over long distances.

I've noticed that recent game releases, like GTA 6 and even this Jurassic Park Survival game, seem to be incorporating a lot of elements associated with political correctness. There's been a shift in the choice of main characters, such as having a female lead. I'm curious about the reasoning behind these decisions. While I understand the importance of diversity and representation, it seems like some of these choices may not be resonating well with audiences. It's interesting to see how the industry navigates the balance between pushing for inclusivity and ensuring the success of their projects. This phenomenon isn't limited to games; even movies, including those with female leads, seem to face challenges in garnering attention. It's a complex topic, and I'm interested to see how different entertainment companies adapt to changing trends

It was thought that there weren‚Äôt anymore on Isla Nublar since the first movie until Jurassic World. Just three theories:  First Theory: From the first film, the unfortunate individual was locked in the freezer by the kids; The Big One and her other subordinate were finished off  by Rexy. Maybe the one in the Freezer had the unbelievable willpower to keep pounding the locked door or if the new protagonist of this new game unintentionally unlocked it out of hunger for if there‚Äôs any food.  Second Theory: From Telltale Game JP of 2011, There was also a new shipment of five Raptors that had been sent in from Site B to replace the original five the Big One killed. Two were taken out: one by Oscar Morales the mercenary and the other by Rexy. Only three, especially the alpha female that was scarred by Oscar are still alive but their whereabouts are unknown. Maybe, just a hope, that those same three raptors from Telltale will appear in this newly, amazing and thrilling game of Jurassic Park. And if the last raptor of the Big One‚Äôs pack escaped the freezer, would come across the new Trio and accept the scarred raptor as her new alpha, making them into four. Four raptors would make things a lot more dangerous and exciting.
